[*[data-tab]_&amp;]:only:border-0 mt-0 border-0"><pre class="shiki github-light h-full"><code>import { createRootRoute, createRoute, createRouter, RouterProvider } from &#x27;@tanstack/react-router&#x27;

const rootRoute = createRootRoute()
const indexRoute = createRoute({
  getParentRoute: () =&gt; rootRoute,
  path: &#x27;/&#x27;,
  component: () =&gt; &lt;div&gt;Hello World&lt;/div&gt;,
})
const routeTree = rootRoute.addChildren([indexRoute])
const router = createRouter({ routeTree })

export default function App() {
  return &lt;RouterProvider router={router} /&gt;
}</code></pre><pre class="shiki vitesse-dark"><code>import { createRootRoute, createRoute, createRouter, RouterProvider } from &#x27;@tanstack/react-router&#x27;

const rootRoute = createRootRoute()
const indexRoute = createRoute({
  getParentRoute: () =&gt; rootRoute,
  path: &#x27;/&#x27;,
  component: () =&gt; &lt;div&gt;Hello World&lt;/div&gt;,
})
const routeTree = rootRoute.addChildren([indexRoute])
const router = createRouter({ routeTree })

export default function App() {
  return &lt;RouterProvider router={router} /&gt;
}</code></pre></div><div class="mt-4 text-center"><a href="/router/llms-full.txt/docs" class="inline-block py-2 px-4 rounded-lg font-black transition-colors bg-emerald-500 text-white">Get Started</a></div></div></div><div class="text-lg grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 xl:grid-cols-3 gap-x-8 gap-y-12 p-8 max-w-[1200px] mx-auto"><div class="bg-white dark:bg-gray-900 shadow-md border border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-800 p-4 pt-6 flex-1 flex flex-col gap-4 items-center rounded-xl relative"><div class="bg-white dark:bg-gray-900 shadow-md border border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-800 text-3xl text-center p-2 rounded-full absolute top-0 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 -translate-y-2/3"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-plug-zap scale-125 text-emerald-500 dark:text-emerald-400" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M6.3 20.3a2.4 2.4 0 0 0 3.4 0L12 18l-6-6-2.3 2.3a2.4 2.4 0 0 0 0 3.4Z"></path><path d="m2 22 3-3"></path><path d="M7.5 13.5 10 11"></path><path d="M10.5 16.5 13 14"></path><path d="m18 3-4 4h6l-4 4"></path></svg></div><div class="flex flex-col gap-4"><h3 class="uppercase text-xl font-black">Typesafe &amp; powerful, yet familiarly simple</h3><div class="text-sm text-gray-800 dark:text-gray-200 leading-6"><div>TanStack Router builds on modern routing patterns made popular by other tools, but has been re-engineered from the ground up to be<!-- --> <span class="font-semibold text-emerald-500 dark:text-emerald-400">100% typesafe without compromising on DX</span>. You <em>can</em> have your cake and eat it too!</div></div></div></div><div class="bg-white dark:bg-gray-900 shadow-md border border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-800 p-4 pt-6 flex-1 flex flex-col gap-4 items-center rounded-xl relative"><div class="bg-white dark:bg-gray-900 shadow-md border border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-800 text-3xl text-center p-2 rounded-full absolute top-0 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 -translate-y-2/3"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-database-zap motion-safe:animate-spin text-emerald-500 dark:text-emerald-400" aria-hidden="true" style="animation-duration:3s;animation-timing-function:ease-in-out"><ellipse cx="12" cy="5" rx="9" ry="3"></ellipse><path d="M3 5V19A9 3 0 0 0 15 21.84"></path><path d="M21 5V8"></path><path d="M21 12L18 17H22L19 22"></path><path d="M3 12A9 3 0 0 0 14.59 14.87"></path></svg></div><div class="flex flex-col gap-4"><h3 class="uppercase text-xl font-black">Built-in Data Fetching with Caching</h3><div class="text-sm text-gray-800 dark:text-gray-200 leading-6"><div>Hoist your data fetching and avoid waterfalls with TanStack Router&#x27;s loader API and get<!-- --> <span class="font-semibold text-emerald-500 dark:text-emerald-400">instant navigations with built-in caching and automatic preloading</span>. Need something more custom? Router&#x27;s API is designed to work with your favorite client-side cache libraries!</div></div></div></div><div class="bg-white dark:bg-gray-900 shadow-md border border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-800 p-4 pt-6 flex-1 flex flex-col gap-4 items-center rounded-xl relative"><div class="bg-white dark:bg-gray-900 shadow-md border border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-800 text-3xl text-center p-2 rounded-full absolute top-0 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 -translate-y-2/3"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-message-circle-question-mark text-emerald-500 dark:text-emerald-400" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M2.992 16.342a2 2 0 0 1 .094 1.167l-1.065 3.29a1 1 0 0 0 1.236 1.168l3.413-.998a2 2 0 0 1 1.099.092 10 10 0 1 0-4.777-4.719"></path><path d="M9.09 9a3 3 0 0 1 5.83 1c0 2-3 3-3 3"></path><path d="M12 17h.01"></path></svg></div><div class="flex flex-col gap-4"><h3 class="uppercase text-xl font-black">Search Param APIs to make your state-manager jealous</h3><div class="text-sm text-gray-800 dark:text-gray-200 leading-6"><div>Instead of throwing you to the URLSearchParam wolves, TanStack Router outfits you with state-manager-grade search param APIs. sync it to your state-manager of choice.</div></div></div></div></div><div class="w-full overflow-hidden py-8"><div class="text-center mb-8 px-4"><h3 class="text-2xl font-black mb-2">Loved by
